Snakes and Ladders is played between two or more players on a game-board having numbered, gridded squares. A number of ladders and snakes are pictured on the board, each connecting two specific board squares. The object of the game is to navigate one's game piece, according to die rolls, from the start to a bottom square and the finish to top square helped or hindered by ladders and snakes respectively.\r\n\r\nEnjoy classic LUDO board game with friends, family & kids.
